The scope is constrained to one complete vertical slice with clean code, documentation, and CI/CD.
Deliverables (MVP thin slice):
App foundation: Next.js 14 (App Router), TypeScript, Tailwind CSS, modular component setup.


Auth: Email/password (or magic link) with session management and protected routes.


Billing: Stripe Checkout subscriptions (1 plan + customer portal link), basic Billing page.


Data model: PostgreSQL schema + migrations for one primary entity (e.g., Projects) with full CRUD.


Dashboard: Responsive dashboard page listing entities with create/edit/delete and basic filtering.


Quality &amp; performance: Lighthouse  90 mobile/desktop on the dashboard route; Core Web Vitals green.


Ops: GitHub repo, GitHub Actions CI, oneclick deploy to Vercel (staging + production), .env template.


Docs &amp; handover: README (setup, run, deploy), short admin guide, and minimal runbook.


Out of scope (this phase): multitenant roles beyond an owner role, complex analytics, internationalization, mobile apps, and advanced reporting.
What to include in your proposal:
35 sentences on your technical approach (auth, billing, data model, CI/CD).


23 links to similar SaaS/Dashboard work (live or GitHub).

      Summary
    </strong> <p data-v-74025d29="" class="text-body-sm">We need an expert fullstack TypeScript developer to deliver a thin-slice SaaS MVP that is productionready and sets a strong foundation for future features. The scope is constrained to one complete vertical slice with clean code, documentation, and CI/CD.<br>
Deliverables (MVP thin slice):<br>
App foundation: Next.js 14 (App Router), TypeScript, Tailwind CSS, modular component setup.<br>
<br>
<br>
Auth: Email/password (or magic link) with session management and protected routes.<br>
<br>
<br>
Billing: Stripe Checkout subscriptions (1 plan + customer portal link), basic Billing page.<br>
<br>
<br>
Data model: PostgreSQL schema + migrations for one primary entity (e.g., Projects) with full CRUD.<br>
<br>
<br>
Dashboard: Responsive dashboard page listing entities with create/edit/delete and basic filtering.<br>
<br>
<br>
Quality &amp; performance: Lighthouse  90 mobile/desktop on the dashboard route; Core Web Vitals green.<br>
<br>
<br>
Ops: GitHub repo, GitHub Actions CI, oneclick deploy to Vercel (staging + production), .env template.<br>
<br>
<br>
Docs &amp; handover: README (setup, run, deploy), short admin guide, and minimal runbook.<br>
<br>
<br>
Out of scope (this phase): multitenant roles beyond an owner role, complex analytics, internationalization, mobile apps, and advanced reporting.<br>
What to include in your proposal:<br>
35 sentences on your technical approach (auth, billing, data model, CI/CD).<br>
<br>
<br>
23 links to similar SaaS/Dashboard work (live or GitHub).<br>
<br>
<br>
Confirmation of experience with Next.js 14 and Stripe subscriptions.<br>
<br>
<br>
A brief milestone plan (foundation  auth/billing  CRUD/dashboard  polish/handover).<br>
<br>
<br>
Your earliest start date and weekly availability.</p> <!----></div></section> <section data-v-6dbef4fa="" data-v-1656f905="" data-ev-sublocation="page" data-ev-label="contract_to_hire_tag_impression" data-ev-label-prefix="" impression="0.5" class="air3-card-section text-base-sm" eh-i="true"><ul data-v-6dbef4fa="" class="features list-unstyled m-0"><!----> <!----> <li data-v-6dbef4fa=""><div data-v-6dbef4fa="" class="air3-icon md" data-cy="fixed-price"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" viewBox="0 0 24 24" role="img"><path vector-effect="non-scaling-stroke" stroke="var(--icon-color, #001e00)" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M13.17 3H21v7.83L10.83 21 3 13.17 13.17 3z"></path><path vector-effect="non-scaling-stroke" stroke="var(--icon-color, #001e00)" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9.63 11.51a1.86 1.86 0 00.3 2.56 1.86 1.86 0 002.56.3 1.51 1.51 0 00.27-1.68c-.25-.54-.87-1.56-1.08-2.12A1.4 1.4 0 0112 9.12a1.84 1.84 0 012.55.31 1.84 1.84 0 01.33 2.57m-.31-2.57l.81-.81m-6.26 6.26l.81-.81m7.94-7.39a.55.55 0 100-1.1.55.55 0 000 1.1z"></path></svg></div> <div data-v-6dbef4fa=""><div data-v-2546b8da="" data-v-6dbef4fa=""><p data-v-2546b8da="" class="m-0"><strong data-v-2546b8da="">
